  <script type="text/javascript">
   var gContextPath = "";
  
$(function() {
	
	

	

	
	
	
	
	/* $("#viewDivisional").click(function(){

	});

	var nPopupWindowCnt = 0;
	

	if(nPopupWindowCnt>0){
		$(".layerPop").show();
		$(".layerPop_bg").show();
	}else{
		$(".layerPop").hide();
	}
	
	// 매트릭스가이드 쿠키로 자동 열기방식에서 도움말 클릭해 열기방식으로 변경
	var nPopupMatrixGuideNum = 1;
	/* 
	$(".layerPop").hide();
	var nPopupMatrixGuideCnt = 0;
	if ( getCookie( "matrixGuide" ) != "done" ){
	
		$(".layerPop").show();
		nPopupMatrixGuideCnt = nPopupMatrixGuideCnt + 1;
	}
	
	//if(nPopupWindowCnt>0 || nPopupMatrixGuideCnt>0){
	if(nPopupMatrixGuideCnt>0){
		$(".layerPop_bg").show();
	} */
	
	$(document).on('click', '.btnPopupWinodwChk', function(){
		var strPopupId = $(this).attr("popupId");
		$("#layerPop"+strPopupId).hide();
		
		 setCookie( "mainPopupId"+strPopupId, "done" , 1);
		 
		 nPopupWindowCnt = nPopupWindowCnt -1;
		 if( nPopupWindowCnt == 0 ){
			 $(".layerPop").hide();
		 }
	});
	
	$(document).on('click', '.btnPopupWinodwClose', function(){
		var strPopupId = $(this).attr("popupId");
		$("#layerPop"+strPopupId).hide();
		
		 nPopupWindowCnt = nPopupWindowCnt -1;
		 if( nPopupWindowCnt == 0 ){
			 $(".layerPop").hide();
		 }
		 
	});
	
	$(document).on('click', '.page_close', function(){
		
		var term = 0;
		
		if($('input:checkbox[name="matixGuideCloseAll"]').is(":checked"))
			 term = 365;
		
		if($('input:checkbox[name="matixGuideCloseDay"]').is(":checked"))
			 term = 1;
		
		$(".layerPop").hide();
		
		if(term > 0){
			setCookie( "matrixGuide", "done" , term);
		}
		
		$(".layerPop_bg").hide();
	});
	/* 
	$("input:checkbox[id=matixGuideCloseAll]").click(function(){
		if($('input:checkbox[name="matixGuideCloseAll"]').is(":checked")){
			 $("input:checkbox[name=matixGuideCloseDay]").prop("checked",false);
		}
	});
	
	$("input:checkbox[name=matixGuideCloseDay]").click(function(){
		if($('input:checkbox[name="matixGuideCloseDay"]').is(":checked")){
			 $("input:checkbox[name=matixGuideCloseAll]").prop("checked",false);
		}
	});
	*/
	
 	$(document).on('click', '#matixGuidePrev', function(){
		
		if(nPopupMatrixGuideNum == 1){
			
			alert("첫번째 페이지입니다.");
			return;
		}
		
		$(".guide01").hide();
		$(".guide02").hide();
		$(".guide03").hide();
		$(".guide04").hide();
	
	 	$("#page_number01").css("display", "none");
		$("#page_number02").css("display", "none");
		$("#page_number03").css("display", "none");
		$("#page_number04").css("display", "none");
	 	
		nPopupMatrixGuideNum = nPopupMatrixGuideNum - 1;
		
		$(".guide0"+nPopupMatrixGuideNum).fadeIn('slow');
		$("#page_number0"+nPopupMatrixGuideNum).css("display", "block");
		
	});
	
	$(document).on('click', '#matixGuideNext', function(){
		
		if(nPopupMatrixGuideNum == 4){
			
			alert("마지막 페이지입니다.");
			return;
		}

		$(".guide01").hide();
		$(".guide02").hide();
		$(".guide03").hide();
		$(".guide04").hide();
		
		$("#page_number01").css("display", "none");
		$("#page_number02").css("display", "none");
		$("#page_number03").css("display", "none");
		$("#page_number04").css("display", "none");
	
		nPopupMatrixGuideNum = nPopupMatrixGuideNum + 1;
		
		$(".guide0"+nPopupMatrixGuideNum).fadeIn('slow');
		$("#page_number0"+nPopupMatrixGuideNum).css("display", "block");
	});
});

function layerPop_close(){
	var term = 0;
	
	if($('input:checkbox[name="matixGuideCloseAll"]').is(":checked"))
		 term = 365;
	
	if($('input:checkbox[name="matixGuideCloseDay"]').is(":checked"))
		 term = 1;
	
	$(".layerPop").hide();
	
	if(term > 0){
		setCookie( "matrixGuide", "done" , term);
	}
	
	$(".layerPop_bg").hide();
}

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var contextUri = ""; 

$(function() {
	
	if( "" != "" && "" != null  && "" != 'guest@khidi.or.kr' ){
		
		var rtn = fnLoginCheck();
	 	if(rtn == 'Fail')
	 	{
		 	alert("현재 다른 기기(브라우저)에서 로그인하였습니다.\n로그아웃 처리하겠습니다.");
	 		$(location).attr('href','/kps/member/nologout?siteId=SITE00002');//로그아웃처리
	 	} 
	}
	
	
		$('.roleWRITE').hide();
	
	
	
		$('.roleMODIFY').hide();
	
	
	
	
	
		$('.roleREAD').hide();
	
	
	// 접근성을 위해 키보드 접근 시 마우스 오버 효과
	$(".khidi_hm > li > a").each(function(){
		if($(this).attr("class").indexOf("on") > -1){
			contextUri = $(this).parent().attr("class");
		}
	});
	
	$(".khidi_hm > li > a").focusin(function(){
		if($(this).attr("class").indexOf("on") == -1){
			$(this).addClass("on");
		}
	});
	
	$(".khidi_hm > li > a").focusout(function(){
		if($(this).parent().attr("class") != contextUri){
			$(this).removeClass("on");
		}
	});
	
});

function fnLoginCheck(){
	
	var returnV = "";		
	$.ajax({
 		url: gContextPath+"kps/member/loginCheck",
 		data: {'kind' : 'P', 'schType' : '0'}, //schType : 0(Dkey 체크)
 		async: false,
		cache: false,
 		success:function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
			if(data != ""){
				if(data == 'F') //최근 아이피, 유저아이디 비고하여 상태가 F일때
				{
					returnV = "Fail"; 
				}
				
			}else{
				returnV = "Sucess";
			}
 		}
 	});
	
	return returnV;
}

function fnLogin(){
	$('#loginForm').submit();
}

$(function() {
	
    var addUrl = location.href;
	
	var resultA = addUrl.indexOf('search/result');
	
	var resultB = addUrl.indexOf('/board');
	
	var resultC = addUrl.indexOf('kps/event');
	
	var resultD = addUrl.indexOf('kps/contentsMap'); 
	
	if(resultA != -1 || resultB != -1 || resultC != -1 || resultD != -1)
	{
		var subUrl = addUrl; 
		
		var resultRtn = addUrl.indexOf('?');
		
		if(resultRtn == -1)
		{
			subUrl = subUrl+ "?";
			subUrl = encodeURI(subUrl);
			$("#rtnUrlLogin").val(subUrl);
		}else{
			addUrl = encodeURI(addUrl);
			$("#rtnUrlLogin").val(addUrl);
		}
	}else
	{
		$("#rtnUrlLogin").val(addUrl);	
	}
	
	$("#viewDivisional").click(function(){
		$('#divisional_area').slideDown("slow");
		$('#divisional_area').animate({opacity: 1}, 600);
		
	});

	$("#closeDivisional").click(function(){
		$("#divisional_area").slideUp("slow");
		$('#divisional_area').animate({opacity: 0}, 600);
		$("#viewDivisional").focus();
	});
	
});

			$(".depth2").css('display', 'none');
			var topMenuId = $(this).attr("id");
			$("#"+topMenuId).next().css('display', 'block');
			
			if($("#gnavigation").children().last().attr("id") == $("#"+topMenuId).parents().attr("id")){
				var pId = $("#gnavigation").children().last().attr("id");
				
				$(".depth2 >li>a").focus(function(){
					if($(this).parents().attr("id") == $("#"+pId+" >ul").children().last().attr("id")){
						$(this).blur(function(){
							$(".depth2").css('display', 'none');
						});
					};
				});
			};
		});
		
		$("#gnavigation > li").hover(function(){
			$(this).children().eq(1).css('display', 'none');
			$(this).children().eq(1).css('display', 'block');
		}, function(){
			$(this).children().eq(1).css('display', 'none');
		});
	});

	document.totSearchForm.searchField.value = objId;
	gfnTotalSearch();
}

	document.totSearchForm.collection.value = objId;
	gfnTotalSearch();
}

function setNavCollection(objId){
	
	document.totSearchForm.collAll.value = objId;
	document.totSearchForm.collection.value = 'ALL';
	
	gfnTotalSearch();
}

function setPeriod(objId){
		
	var startDate;
	var endDate;
	var today = "2018/06/24";
	
	if(objId == ""){
		startDate = "";
		endDate = "";
	}else if(objId == "today"){
		startDate = today;
		endDate = today;
	}else if(objId == "week"){
		startDate = jsDateCalculation(today, objId);
		endDate = today;
	}else if(objId == "month"){
		startDate = jsDateCalculation(today, objId);
		endDate = today;
	}else if(objId == "year"){
		startDate = jsDateCalculation(today, objId);
		endDate = today;
	}else if(objId == "keyIn"){
		startDate = $('#startDate').val();
		endDate = $('#endDate').val();
	}
	
	document.totSearchForm.startDate.value = startDate;
	document.totSearchForm.endDate.value = endDate;
	document.totSearchForm.period.value = objId;
	
	gfnTotalSearch();
}

function goDetailSearch(){
	document.totSearchForm.DETAIL_1.value = $('#DETAIL_1').val();
	document.totSearchForm.DETAIL_2.value = $('#DETAIL_2').val();
	document.totSearchForm.DETAIL_3.value = $('#DETAIL_3').val();
	document.totSearchForm.DETAIL_4.value = $('#DETAIL_4').val();
	
	gfnTotalSearch();
}


/* 날짜계산 */
var jsDateCalculation = function(date, term) {

    var selectDate = date.split("/");
    var changeDate = new Date();

    if( term == 'week' ) {
       // 일주일전
        changeDate.setFullYear(selectDate[0], selectDate[1]-1, selectDate[2]-7);
    }
    if( term == 'month' ) {
       // 한달전
        changeDate.setFullYear(selectDate[0], selectDate[1]-2, selectDate[2]);
    }
    if( term == 'year' ) {
       // 일년전
        changeDate.setFullYear(selectDate[0]-1, selectDate[1]-1, selectDate[2]);
    }
    var y = changeDate.getFullYear();
    var m = changeDate.getMonth() + 1;
    var d = changeDate.getDate();

    if(m < 10) { 
        m = "0" + m;
    }
    if(d < 10) {
        d = "0" + d;
    }
    var resultDate = y + "/" + m + "/" + d;
    return resultDate;
};

function viewSchHistory(){

	makeHistoryList();
}

function getSchCookie(key){
	
	var cook = document.cookie + ";";
	var idx = cook.indexOf(key,0);
	var val = "";
	
	if(idx!=-1)
	{
		cook = cook.substring(idx,cook.length);
		begin = cook.indexOf("=",0) + 1;
		end = cook.indexOf(";",begin);
		val = unescape(cook.substring(begin,end));
	}
	
	return val;
}

function makeHistoryList(){
	$('.search_keyword *').remove();
	
	var $dl = $('.search_keyword');
	$dl.append('<dt>내가 찾은 검색어</dt>');
	
	var html = '<dd>';
	for(var i=1; i <=5; i++){
		if(getCookie("schKeyWord"+i) != ""){
			html += '<a href="#" onclick="javascript:goRecommandSearch(\''+getCookie("schKeyWord"+i)+'\');">'+getCookie("schKeyWord"+i)+'</a>';
		}
	}
	html += '</dd>';
	$dl.append(html);
}

function fnDelHistory(){
	
	viewSchHistory();

	for(var i=1; i <=5; i++){
		if(getCookie("schKeyWord"+i) != ""){
			setCookieWithSamePath("schKeyWord"+i, getCookie("schKeyWord"+i), -1);
		}
	}
}

     <script>
      $(function() {
	$(".btn_search").bind("keyup",function () {
		if($('#divHistory').prop("class") == "history_layer"){
			css = "history_layer display_none";
			$('#divHistory').prop("class", css);
		}
	});
	
	$("#search_keyword").focus(function(){		
		if($('#divHistory').prop("class") == "history_layer"){
			css = "history_layer display_none";
			$('#divHistory').prop("class", css);
		}
	});
	
	// 핫이슈 스크롤링
	var hotIssueScrollingInterval = setInterval("hotIssueScrolling()", 3000);
	var hotIssueHtml = $("#ul_keywordDays").html(); // 핫이슈 html 백업
	
	$(".hotissue_area").on("mouseenter focus", function(){
		clearInterval(hotIssueScrollingInterval);
		$("#ul_keywordDays").html(hotIssueHtml);
	});
	
	$(".hotissue_area").on("mouseleave", function(){
		hotIssueScrollingInterval = setInterval("hotIssueScrolling()", 3000);
	});
	
});

//핫이슈 스크롤링
function hotIssueScrolling(){
	var hotIssue = $("#ul_keywordDays");
	hotIssue.animate({marginTop:"-25px"}, 200, null, function(){
		hotIssue.css("marginTop", "0px").append(hotIssue.find("> li:first"));
	});
}

function goSelectedQuerySearch(objId){
	document.totSearchForm.query.value = objId;
	document.totSearchForm.categoryQuery.value = "";
	document.totSearchForm.categoryUse.value = 'true';
	
	var name = "";
	var addHistory = true;
	var cookieLength = 30;
	
	for(var i=1; i <=cookieLength; i++){
		if(getCookie("schKeyWord"+padDigit(i)) == objId){
			addHistory = false;
		}
	}

	if(addHistory){
		// 검색어 쿠키를 항상 30개로 채워놓는다. 그래야 최근 것부터 01,02,... 순으로 채워넣을 수 있음.
		if(document.cookie.indexOf("schKeyWord")<0){
			for(var i=1; i<=cookieLength; i++){
				setCookieWithSamePath("schKeyWord"+padDigit(i), "null", 30);
			}
		}

		if(name == ""){
			// 항상 1을 남기고 한칸씩  뒤로 밈.
			for(var i=cookieLength; i>1; i--){
				setCookieWithSamePath("schKeyWord"+padDigit(i), getCookie("schKeyWord"+padDigit(i-1)), 30);
			}
			setCookieWithSamePath("schKeyWord"+padDigit(i), getCookie("schKeyWord"+padDigit(i)), -1);
			name = "schKeyWord"+padDigit(i);
		}
		setCookieWithSamePath(name, objId, 30);
	}
	
	document.totSearchForm.submit();
}
     </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function fnRBoardTabMove(rMenuId){
	var rowCnt = 5; // 페이지당 리스트수	
	if( rMenuId != 'MENU00099' && rMenuId != 'MENU00108'){
		
		 $.ajax({
	 		url: gContextPath+"/kps/listRBoard",
	 		data: {'menuId' : rMenuId, 'rowCnt' : rowCnt},
	 		cache: false,
	 		success:function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
	 			if(data != null) {
	 				$("#MENU00101U >").remove();
	 				$("#MENU01108U >").remove();
	 				
	 				if(data != ""){
	 					// 게시판 게시글 조회
	 	 				$.each(data, function(i, item) {
	 	 					// 게시판 게시글 세팅
	 	 					$("#"+rMenuId+"U").append('<li><a href="/board/view?linkId='+item.LINKID+'&menuId='+rMenuId+'">'+item.KNAME+'</a>'
	 						  					   +'<span class="date">'+item.INSTIME+'</span></li>');
	 	 				});	
	 				}else{
	 				    // 게시판 게시글 세팅
	 					$("#"+rMenuId+"U").append('<span> 조회된 데이터가 없습니다. </span>');
	 				}
	 			}
	 		}
	 	}); 	
	}
	
	$(".notice_area").children('.tab_newsArea').removeClass('on');	
	$("#"+rMenuId).addClass('on');
}

//게시판 탭 메뉴 클릭 시(왼쪽 게시판) : 보도자료, 뉴스클리핑
function fnLBoardTabMove(lMenuId){
	var rowCnt = 5; // 페이지당 리스트수
	
	if( lMenuId != 'MENU00100'){	
		$.ajax({
	 		url: gContextPath+"/kps/listLBoard",
	 		data: {'menuId' : lMenuId, 'rowCnt' : rowCnt},
	 		cache: false,
	 		success:function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
	 			if(data != null) {
	 				
	 				$("#MENU00102U >").remove();
	 				
	 				if(data != ""){
 						// 게시판 게시글 조회
 	 	 				$.each(data, function(i, item) {
 	 	 					// 게시판 게시글 세팅
 	 	 					$("#MENU00102U").append('<li><a href="'+item.LINKURL+'" target="_blank" title="새창으로 열림">'+item.KNAME+'</a></li>');
 	 	 				});
	 				}else{
 						$("#MENU00102U").append('<span> 조회된 데이터가 없습니다. </span>');
	 				}
	 			}
	 		}
	 	});
	}
	
	$(".press_area").children('.tab_newsArea').removeClass('on');
	$("#listLBoard"+lMenuId).addClass('on');
	
}

//선호주제 설정저장시
function fnFixingSubject() {
	var inputVal = $('input:radio[name=indata]:checked').val();
	$.cookie('FixPreferSubject', inputVal);
	location.reload();
}

//선호주제 설정초기화
function fnFixingClose(){
	$(".subject_setting").hide();
	$(".btn_stageSet button").focus();
	
	$.cookie('FixPreferSubject', "");
	location.reload();
}

function fnMoreMatrix(flag){ //매트릭스 더보기/닫기 버튼 클릭했을때
	if(flag == 'more'){
		$(".stage01_l").attr('class','stage01_l stage01_l_on1');	
	}else if(flag == 'close'){
		$(".stage01_l").attr('class','stage01_l');
	}
}

function fnOption(flag){ //매트릭스 설정/닫기 버튼 클릭했을때
	if(flag == 'open'){
		$(".stage01_l").attr('class','stage01_l stage01_l_on2');
		$(".stage01_l_s2").attr('class','stage01_l_s2');
	}else if(flag == 'close'){
		$(".stage01_l").attr('class','stage01_l');	
		$(".stage01_l_s2").attr('class','stage01_l_s2 display_none'); 
	}
}

}

}

function fnKeywordChg(key){
	if(key == "days"){
		$('#keywordWeek').removeClass();
		$('#keywordDays').addClass("on");
		$('#ul_keywordDays').show();
		$('#ul_keywordWeek').hide();
	}else{
		$('#keywordDays').removeClass();
		$('#keywordWeek').addClass("on");
		$('#ul_keywordDays').hide();
		$('#ul_keywordWeek').show();
	}
}

function multiOpen(multiUrl){
	var url = multiUrl.split("§§");
	
	for(var i=0; i<url.length; i++){
		window.open(url[i]);
	}
}

	$('#liTitZone0').focus();
}

	$('.layer_banner').hide();
}

function fnGoDetail(eventUrl, eventId){
	//행사클릭 수 증가
	$.ajax({
		type: 'post',
		url: gContextPath+"/kps/event/addHitcount",
		data: {'eventId' : eventId},
		success:function(data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
			
		}
	});
	
	// 특정 이벤트 클릭 시 본문이동이 아닌 파일다운로드제공 기능
	if(eventUrl.indexOf(",") > -1){
		//var targetUrl = eventUrl.split(",", "2")[0];
		var fileUrl = eventUrl.split(",", "2")[1];
		window.location = fileUrl;
	// end 특정 이벤트 클릭 시 본문이동이 아닌 파일다운로드제공 기능
		
	}else{
		window.open(eventUrl,'_blank');
	}

}

//검색체계 선택 전체 취소
function initMatrix(){
	$(".Matrix_checked").prop("checked", "");
	$(".custom-check").removeClass("checked");
}

// 검색체계 설정저장시
function matrixAction(mode){
	
	var form = $("#matrixForm");
	var chlen = $("input[name='SelSearchcode[]']:checkbox:checked", form).length;
	
	if (chlen == 0){
		if(!confirm("아무 검색체계도 선택되지 않았습니다. 계속하겠습니까?")) {
			return;
		}
	}
	
	var inputGRVal = new Array();
	
	if(mode == 'U'){
		inputGRVal.push("0"+"|"+"0"); //삭제하기 위한 파라미터
	}
	
	$("input[name='SelSearchcode[]']:checked", "form[name=matrixForm]").each(function(){
		inputGRVal.push($(this).val());	
	});

	$('#inputGRVal').val(inputGRVal);

	if(!confirm("저장하시겠습니까?")){
		return;
	}

	if(mode == 'U'){
		$("#matrixForm").submit();
	}else if(mode == 'G'){
		$.cookie('SearchCodeList', null,  { path: '/' }); //기존 쿠키 제거
		$.cookie('SearchCodeList', inputGRVal);
		location.reload();
	}
}

$(function(){
	$(".btn_guide button").click(function(){
		$(".matrix_guide").show();
		return false;
	});	
	$("#Guide-Close").click(function(){
		$(".matrix_guide").hide();
		$(".btn_guide").focus();
		return false;
	});
	
	$("#goodSet").click(function(){
		$(".matrix_setting").show();
		$("#matrixForm input[type='checkbox']").eq(0).focus();
		return false;
	});	
	$("#matrixClose").click(function(){
		$(".matrix_setting").hide();
		$("#goodSet").focus();
		return false;
	});
	
	$(".btn_viewOption > button").click(function(){	

		var length =$("#matrixlength").val();
		
		if(length>0){
			if($(this).children('span').hasClass('viewShow')){
				$(this).children('span').text('한줄 닫기');
				$(this).children('span').attr('class', 'viewClose');
				$(".one_lineMore").show();
				
				var cnt = 0;
				$(".matrix_list > .list_inner").each(function(i){
					if($(this).css("display") == "none" && cnt < 4){
						$(this).show();
						cnt++;
					}
				});
			}else{
				$(this).children('span').text('한줄 더보기');
				$(this).children('span').attr('class', 'viewShow');
				$(".one_lineMore").hide();
				
				$(".matrix_list > .list_inner").hide();
				var cnt = 0;
				$(".matrix_list > .list_inner").each(function(i){
					if($(this).css("display") == "none" && cnt < 8){
						$(this).show();
						cnt++;
					}
				});
			}
		}else{
			alert("설정된 분류체계로 조회된 정보가 존재하지 않습니다.");
		}
	});
			
	$(".one_lineMore > button").click(function(){
		var hiddenLength = $(".matrix_list > .list_inner:hidden").length;
		if(hiddenLength==0){
			$(".one_lineMore").hide();
			$(".one_lineMoreClose").show();
		}else{
			var cnt = 0;
			$(".matrix_list > .list_inner").each(function(i){
				if($(this).css("display") == "none" && cnt < 4){
					$(this).show();
					cnt++;
				}
			});
		}
	});
	
	$(".one_lineMoreClose > button").click(function(){
		$(".one_lineMoreClose").hide();
		$(".btn_viewOption > button").children('span').text('한줄 더보기');
		$(".btn_viewOption > button").children('span').attr('class', 'viewShow');
		
		$(".matrix_list > .list_inner").hide();
		var cnt = 0;
		$(".matrix_list > .list_inner").each(function(i){
			if($(this).css("display") == "none" && cnt < 8){
				$(this).show();
				cnt++;
			}
		});
		
		$('html, body').animate({
            scrollTop: $(".viewShow").offset().top
        }, 300);
	});
	
});

function popup_areaSlide(){
	var param = $(".popup_area");
	var obj = param.find(".popup_list > li");
	var btn = param.find(".btn_control > button");
	var number = param.find(".number");
	var elem = 0;
	var rel = "play";
	var movement;
	var duration = 500;
	var method = "easeInOutCubic";
	var stop = btn.parent().find("[id=Popup-Stop]");
	var play = btn.parent().find("[id=Popup-Start]");
	// 넘버링
	$.each(obj,function(e){
		if(e == elem){
			number.append('<a class="num on" href="#popup_item'+(e+1)+'">'+(e+1)+'</a>');
		}else{
			$(this).css({opacity:1});
			number.append('<a class="num" href="#popup_item'+(e+1)+'">'+(e+1)+'</a>');	
		}
		$(this).attr("id","popup_item"+(e+1));
	});

	// 넘버링
	$(document).ready(function(){
		number.find("a").bind("click",function(event){
			clearInterval(movement); 
			var t = $(this);
			var current = $("[id=popup_item"+(t.index()+1)+"]"); // 현재 index 찾기.

			if(elem != t.index()){
				elem = t.index();
				targetobj = $("[id*=popup_item]:lt("+current.index()+")"); // 현재 이하 반환.
				obj.css({opacity:1});
				obj.parent().stop(true,false).animate({left:current.position().left*-1},100,function(){
					$.each(targetobj,function(e){ // 현재 이하 뒤로, 순서대로 붙임.
						obj.parent().append($(this).detach());
					});
					obj.parent().css({left:0});
				});
				init_numbering();
			}
			return false;
		});
	});

	function init_numbering(){
		number.find("a").not(elem).removeClass("on").eq(elem).addClass("on");
	}
	function init_movement(){
		if(rel == "stop"){
		}
		if(rel == "play"){
			if(elem < obj.size()-1) elem++; else elem = 0;

			obj.parent().stop(true,false).animate({left:(obj.eq(elem).outerWidth())*-1},100,function(){
				obj.parent().append(obj.eq(elem).prev().detach());
				obj.parent().css({left:0});
			});
			
			obj.eq(elem).prev().stop(true,false).animate(100);
			obj.eq(elem).stop(true,false).animate(100);
			init_numbering();
		}
	}
	function autoSlide(){
	 	movement = setInterval(function(){
			init_movement();
		},3000);
	}

	btn.bind("click",function(event){
		clearInterval(movement);
		
		/*
		if($(this).attr("rel") == 'play'){
			document.getElementById("Popup-Stop").style.display = "inline-block";
			document.getElementById("Popup-Start").style.display = "none";
			autoSlide();
		}else{
			document.getElementById("Popup-Stop").style.display = "none";
			document.getElementById("Popup-Start").style.display = "inline-block";
		}
		*/
		event.preventDefault();
	});
	
	obj.find("a").bind("focusin",function(){
		clearInterval(movement);
		rel = "stop";
		init_movement();
		return false;
	});
	autoSlide();
}

//보건산업동향 bxslider
$(document).ready(function(){
	 
	var slider = $('.trend_info').bxSlider({
		  auto: true,
		  autoControls: true,
		  pagerType: 'short',
		  infiniteLoop: false,
		  maxSlides: 3,
		  minSlides: 3,
		  moveSlides:3,
		  slideWidth: 165,
		  slideMargin: 10,
		  speed: 1000,
		  pause: 5000	    
	});
	
});
    </script>

&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;칠레 공공보건청&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(ISP)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;는 의료기기산업협회와 통관&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;세관&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;현재 진행 중인 새로운 처리 시스템&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(CDA, Certificate of Industry Association)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;을 통한 의료기기 수입절차에 엄격한 감시 예정&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;위와 같은 사항은 현재까지 위생 등록 조건이 필요하지 않은 모든 의료기기도 포함되는 사항으로&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;,&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;칠레 공공보건청과 세관&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(National Customs Service) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;간에 이루어지는 절차임&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;* Instituto de Salud Publica(ISP) : &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;칠레 공공보건청 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;- (&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;목적&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;칠레 자국 내 보건수준 증진을 위한 기술적&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&amp;middot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;행정적 지원 제공 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;- (&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;주요업무&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;전염병의 예방 및 감시&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;환경 및 산업보건 증진&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의약품 품질 관리 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;※ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;공공보건청 내 의약품&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&amp;middot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의료기기 인허가 담당 부서&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(ANAMED)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;를 신설&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(&amp;lsquo;12&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;공공보건청&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(ISP)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;은 현재까지 수량&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;품종&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;출처 등의 통제가 없는 시스템을 보완하기 위해 엄격한 감시를 오는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;7&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;일부터 시작할 예정으로&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;새로운 처리 시스템 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&amp;ldquo;Certificate of Industry Association(CDA)&amp;rdquo;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에 대한 상세한 내용은 다음 링크에서 확인 가능 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href="http://giconaweb.ispch.gob.cl/"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href="http://giconaweb.ispch.gob.cl/"&gt;http://giconaweb.ispch.gob.cl/&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[Chile, ISP, 2018.06.19.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://www.ispch.cl/noticia/25503"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href="http://www.ispch.cl/noticia/25503"&gt;http://www.ispch.cl/noticia/25503&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;의료 및 통계&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;아마존 원주민 의료 확산 및 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의료 통계조사를 위한 협회 창립&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&amp;rdquo;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;대부분 중남미 국가들이 많이 겪고 있는 문제 중 하나가&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의료서비스를 받지 못하는 인구에 대한 통계률 집계이며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;특히 아마존 지역을 끼고 있는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;3&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;개국&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;브라질&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;콜롬비아 및 페루&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;는 아마존 지역 주민들의 의료서비스 분배의 형평성으로 인하여 당국에서는 많은 고민을 하고 있는 실정&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;위와 같은 현실에서&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;브라질은 아마존 원주민의 의료서비스 확산 및 통계조사를 위한 연구 및 협회 창설을 통한 아마존 원주민들의 의료&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;특히 여성산모 건강 증진에 적극 나설 예정 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;* &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;오스왈도크르즈와의 파트너십을 통해 대중보건관행 및 생활네트워크&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Redes Vivas e Praticas Populares de Saude) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;프로젝트&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;위와 같은 의료서비스는 아마존 주민들의 의료서비스 형성성 개선뿐아니라&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;통계집계를 통한 향후 의료서비스 질 개선에도 활용될 예정 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;브라질은 원주민 건강 국가정책&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(PNASPI)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에 의해 원주민 건강 특별주의 사무국&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(SESAI)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;을 운영 중에 있으며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;사무국의 역할은 토착민들의 건강증진 및 통계 자료수집을 통한 향후 건강증진 방향성 제시&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;* PANASPI(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;원주민 건강국가정책&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, Politica Nacional de Atencao a Saude dos Povos Indigena)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[Brazil, Ministerio de Saude, 2018&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;6&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;18&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;일&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://portalms.saude.gov.br/noticias/sesai/43586-dsei-alto-rio-solimoes-realiza-oficinas-com-parteiras-tradicionais"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href="http://portalms.saude.gov.br/noticias/sesai/43586-dsei-alto-rio-solimoes-realiza-oficinas-com-parteiras-tradicionais"&gt;http://portalms.saude.gov.br/noticias/sesai/43586-dsei-alto-rio-solimoes-realiza-oficinas-com-parteiras-tradicionais&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;0&quot; style=&quot;line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;ADSI&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;는 제약&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;&amp;middot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;바이오&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;화장품&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;식품분야에 친환경적 재료를 사용해 다양한 연구 추진&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;0&quot; style=&quot;line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;ADSI&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;는 지난 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;2017&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;년도부터 카자흐스탄 업체인 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;'Fitoleum'&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;과 협력하며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;독일기업인 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;Bionorica SE&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;의 독점파트너다&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;0&quot; style=&quot;line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;[Pharmnews, 2018. 6. 15.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;0&quot; style=&quot;text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://pharmnews.kz/ru/news/podpisan-memorandum-o-sotrudnichestve-s-avstriyskim-institutom-skrininga-lekarstvennyh-sredstv_13797&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;http://pharmnews.kz/ru/news/podpisan-memorandum-o-sotrudnichestve-s-avstriyskim-institutom-skrininga-lekarstvennyh-sredstv_13797&quot;&gt;http://pharmnews.kz/ru/news/podpisan-memorandum-o-sotrudnichestve-s-avstriyskim-institutom-skrininga-lekarstvennyh-sredstv_13797&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;0&quot; style=&quot;text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;0&quot; style=&quot;text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;&quot;&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class=&quot;0&quot; style=&quot;line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;Philips - Skolkovo &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;과학 기술 연구소 의료연구협력 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;MOU &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;체결의 일환으로 연구소의 우수학생들은 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;년&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;6&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;개월동안 스콜코보의 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;Phillips Research&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;에서 유급 인턴쉽 과정 수령 가능&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;0&quot; style=&quot;line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;Phillips Research&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;는 디지털헬스케어를 위해 인턴쉽 과정에서 정보 분석&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;예측&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;실용의료기술 개발&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;다양한 바이오기술 접목 등 의료 발전에 큰 관심을 두고 있음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class=&quot;0&quot; style=&quot;line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;&quot;&gt;[TechFusion, 2018. 5. 31.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;6&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;4&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;일&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;), UAE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;샤르자대학병원과 힘찬병원은 샤르자대학병원 내 척추 및 관절 치료 서비스 제공에 관한 협약을 체결함 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;동 협약에 따라 두 병원은 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에 힘찬병원 전문 분야인 재활 치료 관련 척추 및 관절 최소침습수술 도입에 협력키로 하였으며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;특히 최소침습수술은 일반 수술과 비교 입원 기간 감소&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;높은 성공률&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;높은 환자 만족도가 기대됨 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;샤르자대학병원 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;CEO &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;알리 오바이드 알 알리는 금번 힘찬병원과의 협력이 샤르자의 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;GCC&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;와 중동 및 북아프리카 지역 프리미엄 헬스케어 목적지로서의 입지를 한층 강화시킬 것이라고 전함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;힘찬병원 이수찬 원장은 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;선두 의료기관인 샤르자대학병원과의 협력은 힘찬병원의 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;진출의 첫 발을 내딛는 계기가 될 것이라고 밝힘 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;힘찬병원은 척추 및 관절 수술 전문 병원으로 종합적인 진단&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;수술 등 치료 서비스를 제공하며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;무릎부터 요추&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;발목&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;발&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;어깨&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;고관절&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;체형교정에 이르는 관절 치료를 위한 전문 의료 시스템을 갖추고 있음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;최근 사우디아라비아 여행을 다녀온 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;가야티 지역 낙타농장을 운영하는 이 환자는 열&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;기침&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;호흡곤란&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;고혈압&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;간질성 폐질환 증상을 앓아 병원을 찾았으며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;검사결과 메르스 양성반응을 최종 확인함 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2012&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;9&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월 이후 세계적으로 메르스 확진 건은 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;787&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;명 사망 포함 총 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2,207&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;건으로&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, 2018&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년에는 현재까지 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;오만&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;말레이시아 각 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;건과 사우디아라비아 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;13&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;건으로 총 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;16&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;건의 메르스가 발생함 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[Khaleejtimes, 2018. 5. 29]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;의료서비스&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;개정되는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;UAE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;보건규정&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;여성의 배아 냉동 허용&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2012&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;연방국가위원회는 배아 냉동을 금지했고 이에 따라 모든 배아 냉동은 보건부의 특별허가가 필요했으나&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;앞으로 항암치료나 약물치료로 인해 가임 기능이 손상된 여성은 특별허가 없이 배아 냉동이 허용됨&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;미혼여성의 배아 냉동에는 여전히 몇 가지 규제 사항이 유지될 것으로 예상되지만 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;35&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;세 이상 미혼여성의 배아 냉동은 허용될 가능성이 높음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;전체 가정의 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;30~35%&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;가 어떤 형태든 불임 문제를 겪고 있으며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, UAE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;출생률은 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2009&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;3.7&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에서 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2014&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;3.4&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;로 감소했음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;규정 개정으로 배아 냉동 시술을 위한 해외 의료관광은 감소하고&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, UAE&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;내 난임치료 수요는 증가할 것으로 예상됨&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[The National, 2018. 5. 22]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: left; line-height: 180%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); text-align: left; line-height: 180%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;보건의료정책&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;아부다비 보건청&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;, UAE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;최초로 인공지능 규정 도입&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;아부다비 보건청이 인공지능 사용에 대한 규정을 도입함에 따라&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;아부다비에 등록된 모든 의료공급자&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;제약사&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;연구자&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;보험회사는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;AI &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;관련 규정을 따라야 함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;모하메드 알 하멜리 아부다비 보건청장은 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;AI&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;가 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;보건산업 성장의 올바른 방향이라 언급하며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, AI &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;사용 관련 규정 시행이 최상의 의료서비스 제공과 더불어 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;AI&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;시장에서 아부다비의 입지를 강화할 것이라 말함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;AI&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;산업은 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2035&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년까지 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에 미화 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;1800&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;억 달러&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;한화 약&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;194&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;조&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;규모의 경제 이득을 가져올 것으로 전망되며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;금융업 다음으로 보건산업이 가장 큰 수혜자가 될 것임&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[The National, 2018. 5. 28]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;올여름 장기기증 등록 프로그램 시작을 앞두고 의료관계자와 시민들 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;1,000&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;여명이 모인 가운데 장기기증 등록 프로그램 참여를 장려하는 워크숍이 아부다비에서 열렸음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2016&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 장기이식이 합법화된 이후 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;22&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;명의 환자가 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;6&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;명의 기증자로부터 장기이식을 받았으나&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, UAE&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의 장기 기증 건은 여전히 매우 저조한 편임&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;장기이식 등록 프로그램 도입은 아직 초기 단계이며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;장기이식 등록 정보는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;UAE&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의 신분증인 에미리츠 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;ID&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;카드와 연결될 것임&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;국가장기이식위원회의 알 오베들리박사는 한 명의 장기 기증자가 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;8&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;명의 환자를 살릴 수 있다고 언급하며 장기이식의 장려와 함께 장기부전 예방의 중요성 또한 강조하였음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;보건의료정책&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;쿠웨이트 보건부 장관&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;, KD 1,000&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;만 이상 규모 입찰 건 취소&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;쿠웨이트 보건부 장관 셰이크 바셀 알 사바는 보건부 산하 시설 관련 입찰 과정에서의 부정을 보고받은 이후 총 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;KD 1,000&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;만&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;한화 약 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;356&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;억&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;규모 이상인 다수의 입찰 건 취소를 지시함 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;쿠웨이트 보건부 장관은 앞서 보건부 산하 시설 관련 모든 입찰&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;관행&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;직접 주문 건들에 대한 검토 지시를 내린바 있으며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;조사 결과 계약체결 없이 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;3&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 승인된 건들과 몇몇 입찰 건은 대체 가능한 것이 밝혀짐&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[KuwaitTimes, 2018. 6. 3.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://news.kuwaittimes.net/website/health-minister-cancels-tenders-worth-kd-10-million/"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href="http://news.kuwaittimes.net/website/health-minister-cancels-tenders-worth-kd-10-million/"&gt;http://news.kuwaittimes.net/website/health-minister-cancels-tenders-worth-kd-10-million/&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;질병정보&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;3&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;번째 콜레라 물결&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;예멘 위협&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;유니세프&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;런던위생열대의대&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;존스홉킨스의대&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;파스퇴르연구소&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, WHO, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;예멘보건부 등이 참여한 연구조사에 따르면&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, 4&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월 시작된 장마철이 끝나면 예멘에서 수백만 명이 콜레라에 감염될 것이라 예상함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2016&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년과 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2017&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 연속적으로 발생한 콜레라 확산은 올해 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;3&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월을 기준으로 감소하는 추세였지만&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;추가 확산이 예상됨에 따라 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;WHO&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;40&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;만명 분의 콜레라 백신을 확보한 상태이나&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;콜레라가 창궐할 경우 모든 환자를 치료하기에는 부족한 양임&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;예멘 전체 인구의 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;72%&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;는 안전한 상수도 공급을 받지 못하고 있으며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, 2016&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년부터 콜레라 환자로 예상되는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2,200&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;명이 사망하였음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[Science and Development Network, 2018. 5. 30]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.scidev.net/global/disease/news/cholera-third-wave-threatens-yemen.html"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;https://www.scidev.net/global/disease/news/cholera-third-wave-threatens-yemen.html&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;의료서비스&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;바레인 아라비안걸프대학&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;, 2&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;억 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;6,600&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;만 달러 메디컬시티 건설 준비 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;바레인 아라비안걸프대학&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(AGU:Arabian Gulf University)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에 따르면 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;억 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;6,600&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;만 달러 규모의 메디컬시티 건설 준비 작업이 완료 단계에 있음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;사우디아라비아 선왕 압둘라 빈 압둘아지즈 알 사우드는 바레인에 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;억 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;6,600&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;만 달러 투자를 통한 아라비안걸프대학 부속 메디컬시티 설립을 지시했으며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;바레인 국왕 하마드 빈 이사 알 칼리파는 이 프로젝트를 위해 수도 마나마 남쪽 지역 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;100&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;만 평방미터 대지를 기부하였음 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이 대형 프로젝트는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;300&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;병상 규모로 종합 외래 클리닉&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, 15&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;개 수술실 및 당뇨&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;비만&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;암&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;심혈관 질환 중심의 임상연구센터를 갖출 것임 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.1pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;아라비안걸프대학 총장 칼리드 압둘 라흐만 알 오할리는 메디컬시티 건설 시공 계약자 공고를 포함한 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;단계에 진입할 준비가 되었으며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이 프로젝트를 통해 국제적 수준의 의료서비스 제공 목표를 성취할 것으로 기대된다고 전함 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[BahrainBusinessNews, 2018. 6. 11.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -10.4pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 5pt; margin-left: 10.4pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-hansi-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&amp;lt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;통지&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&amp;gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;주요 내용 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;table style="border-right-color: currentColor; border-bottom-color: currentColor; border-left-color: currentColor; border-right-width: medium; border-bottom-width: medium; border-left-width: medium; border-right-style: none; border-bottom-style: none; border-left-style: none; border-collapse: collapse; mso-table-overlap: never;"&gt;
