&lt;td valign="middle" style="padding: 1.41pt 5.1pt; border: 0.28pt solid rgb(0, 0, 0); border-image: none; width: 471.03pt; height: 220.82pt;"&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.5pt; margin-left: 25.5pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt; &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-hansi-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;▶ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기구내 활동하는 의약대표 관련 규정 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.7pt; margin-left: 25.7pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의약대표는 의료기구 진료실&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;입원실&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;검사실&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기기실&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;물품실&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;정보관리부문 등 주요지역내에서 활동 금지&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.1pt; margin-left: 25.1pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기구 지정부문 내에서 의약대표는 해당 의약품 생산경영기업의 정보&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;유관 의약품 정보&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;유관업무 수행원 개인정보 등에 대해 등록 필요&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.5pt; margin-left: 25.5pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기구는 비안등록한 의약대표에게 업무용 명찰을 지급하고 의약대표는 의료기구내에서 반드시 업무용 명찰 착용 필요&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.4pt; margin-left: 25.4pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기구 관계자&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&amp;middot;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의약대표 간 면담시 반드시 사전 면담시간&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;면담장소&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;면담인원을 지정하고 면담기록 및 보유&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;또 의료기구 내 면담절차를 수립하여 절차에 따라 엄격히 실행&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.5pt; font-size: 5pt; margin-left: 25.5pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt; &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-hansi-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;▶ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의약대표를 대응하는 의료기구 관련 규정&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.6pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; margin-left: 25.6pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기구내 점검팀을 구성하여 매일 비정기적으로 순찰 시행&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;지정된 시간 및 장소 외에서 의약대표 활동 발견 시 활동증거 확보 및 보고하고 의약대표 불량신용 기록내 등록&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.3pt; margin-left: 25.3pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기구 주요지역 내 설치한 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;CCTV&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;자료는 최소 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;90&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;일 보류하고 의료기구 내 의약대표 활동정보에 대해 기록 및 관리&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -16.4pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 5pt; margin-left: 16.4pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-text-raise: 0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;外购药品&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; vertical-align: super; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;*&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;을 처방 시&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;특정 약국 혹은 의료기관으로 유도하는 행위 금지&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -19.3pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-left: 19.3pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;* &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;외부구입의약품 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;의료기구 의약품판매목록 내 포함되어 있지 않아 의료기구 외부에서 구입이 필요하는 의약품&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;제품&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -15.9pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 5pt; margin-left: 15.9pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-hansi-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;의료기구 의약품판매목록 내 대체 가능한 의약품이 없고 질병치료에 반드시 필요할 경우에만 의료진은 외부구입의약품 처방이 가능&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;외부구입의약품 처방 시 환자들에게 상세한 의약품 설명이 필요하고 의약품 사용에 대한 서면동의서를 받아야함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;또 의료기구에서는 매 월 의료진들의 외부구입의약품 처방 내역을 공개 정리하여 이상점 발견 시 해당 의료진에 대해 조사 진행&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -19.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-left: 19.4pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;[5/22, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;베이징국가정부망&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -20.2pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-left: 20.2pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://www.beijing.gov.cn/bmfw/wsfw/ggts/t1524657.htm?from=timeline"&gt;&lt;u style="text-underline: #0000ff single;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;u style="text-underline: #0000ff single;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://www.beijing.gov.cn/bmfw/wsfw/ggts/t1524657.htm?from=timeline"&gt;http://www.beijing.gov.cn/bmfw/wsfw/ggts/t1524657.htm?from=timeline&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -16.5pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 5pt; margin-left: 16.5pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; &lt;td valign="middle" style="padding: 1.41pt 5.1pt; border: 0.28pt solid rgb(0, 0, 0); border-image: none; width: 468.2pt; height: 204.82pt;"&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.5pt; margin-left: 25.5pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt; &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-hansi-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;▶ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기구내 감염관리팀 설립&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.2pt; margin-left: 25.2pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;감염관리팀은 의료기구 내 감염관리에 대한 업무를 수행하고 감염관리에 관한 제도&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;계획&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;조치&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;절차 등에 대해 수립&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;또 의료기구 내 의료진 및 환자에게 감염관리 관련 대처방법 및 유관 지식 전달 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.5pt; margin-left: 25.5pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt; &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-hansi-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;▶ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;감염관리 관련 인원교육 실시&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;감염관리 관련 설비 준비 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.2pt; margin-left: 25.2pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료진은 의료기구내 감염관리 지식 및 대처방법에 대한 교육을 참여하고 의료기구내 감염관리 관련 제도 및 절차에 대해 숙지 필요&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기구는 체온계&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;위생기구&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;살균제품 등 감염관리를 위한 물품 및 설비 구비 필요 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.5pt; margin-left: 25.5pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt; &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-hansi-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;▶ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;사전 검사 진료제도 설립 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.2pt; margin-left: 25.2pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;각 의료기구는 해당 의료기구 서비스 현황에 맞는 사전 검사 진료제도 수립 필요&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;. 2&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;급이상 종합병원은 별도의 감염질병관리과 설립이 필요하고&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;별도의 감염질병관리과 설립이 불가한 의료기구는 별도의 전염병 사전 검사 및 진료실 준비 및 환자안내를 통해 전염병 확산 방지 및 치료 강화&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;/tbody&gt;
&lt;/table&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -10.4pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 5pt; margin-left: 10.4pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;!--[if !supportEmptyParas]--&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;!--[endif]--&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -25.5pt; margin-left: 25.5pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;- &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;정부에서 의료기구 감염관리 능력 및 수준에 대해 평가 시 의료기구 감염관리팀 운영현황&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;감염 예방 및 관리 교육수준&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;의료기구 내 감염정도 측정&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-ascii-font-family: 한양중고딕; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;font face="굴림"&gt;, &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="mso-fareast-font-family: 한양중고딕;"&gt;감염 예방 및 관리 대처능력 등을 기준으로 참고 예정&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

&lt;p class="0" style="text-indent: -20.2pt; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-left: 20.2pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;의료기관&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 휴먼명조; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; mso-ascii-font-family: 휴먼명조; mso-font-width: 100%; mso-text-raise: 0pt;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 휴먼명조;"&gt;국가의료보장국 신설&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -15.8pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 5pt; margin-left: 15.8pt; mso-pagination: none; mso-padding-alt: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0pt; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>(Medicaid expansion)</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>으로 인해 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>1</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>천</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>5</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>백</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>1</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>십만명 이상이 의료보험을 받았음</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>이들 중 다수는 전에는 메디케이드 수혜자가 아니었음</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>즉 프로그램 확대에 따라 주정부도 동일 레벨의 연방</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>/</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>주 프로그램에 예산을 배정하기 위해 노력했음</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. 2005</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>년부터 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>2015</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>년 사이에 예산 지출비율에 있어서 가장 높은 동력이 의료분야인데</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>수치로는 연간 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>5,860</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>억 달러에서부터 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>9,290</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>억달러로 의료예산이 증가했음</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.5pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>▪ </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>의료분야 예산 폭증과 더불어 베이비부머세대</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>(1940</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>년</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>주정부는 균형예산을 위해 노력 중</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>피치 예측치에 따르면 의료와 사회서비스분야 예산은 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>2015</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>년 전체 예산 상 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>30.7%</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>를 차지했지만</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>캘리포니아</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>코네티컷</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>루지애나</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>뉴저지와 펜실베니아 등의 주는 상황이 더 좋지 않음</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>가장 먼저</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>켄터키주는 이미 메디케이드 지출을 줄이기 위해 노동 요건을 변경하는 정책을 시행하고 있음</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>노동 요건이외에도 등록자 수를 줄이기 위하여 수혜 조건 포기</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>(</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>소급 적용 커버리지 낮춤</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>10</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>년 시나리오 분석을 했는데</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>이는 의료와 연금 비용이 향후 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>7</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>년간 예산에 어떤 영향을 줄 것인지를 파악하기 위함</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. 2025</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>년까지 예산을 늘리려면 세금을 올리거나 메디케이드 또는 다른 프로그램 지출을 줄여야 하는데 주요 공교육과 수송분야가 공격분야가 될 것으로 예상</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>[Healthcaredive, 2018.6.14.]</span></p><p class=0 style=text-align: left; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>1</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>상을 마친 시험약에 접근할 수 있도록 시험약 생산자와 직접 거래할 수 있도록 함</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>미 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>규정</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, Q&amp;A </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>등을 포함하는 제안을 준비 중이라고 함</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>.</span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>▪ </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>신설 연방법률의 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>FDA </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>채택과 제도화는 찬반양론을 모두 고려하면서 진행할 것이므로 당분간 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>FDA</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>의 계획은 명확하게 드러나지 않을 것임</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>현재 라첼 셔먼이 주도하에 현재 워킹그룹을 만들어 운영하고 있는데</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>컨설팅 사무소</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>제약과 바이오직스 센타 등의 대표들도 그룹 안에 포함될 것</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. FDA</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>는 이 법률 하에서의 시험약의 사용과 관련된 임상결과치를 사용해서 승인을 지연하거나 하는 등 실제 승인에 영향을 끼치게 하지는 않을 것임</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>물론 그 결과치가 약의 안전성 또는 스폰서의 사용 요청을 결정하는데 중요한 경우라면 달라질 수 있음</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>▪ </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>췌장암 환자를 위한 임상시험약을 가진 중소기업은 실제로 이 법에 따른 접근에 대한 문의를 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>10</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>통이나 받았다고 함</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>관련 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>2</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>개 중소기업은 회사의 시험약을 새로운 연방법 하에서 사전 접근을 부여하지 않을 것이라 함</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>현재 상황에서는 기업의 최종 목표와도 일치하지 않고 그럴 필요성도 못 느끼기 때문</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>.</span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>▪ </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>CDER(Center for Drug Evaluation and Research) </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>직원들도 이에 대한 대응 교육을 받고 있으나 현재까지 실질적인 도움이 되고 있지는 않다</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>왜냐하면 론 존슨</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>(Ron Johnson) </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>상원위원의 발언에 따르면</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>이 신법은 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>FDA</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>에 추가로 더 권한을 주는 법이 아니라 환자들에게 생명에 대한 희망을 주기위해 오히려 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>FDA </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>권한을 축소하는 것이기 때문</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>.</span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 107%; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;>FDA, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;>오피오이드 위기 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;>(Opioid Crisis) </span><span style=font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;>대응을 위한 의료기기 혁신 과제의 수행 개시</span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>▪ </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>미국에서는 매일 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>115</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>명이 넘는 사람들이 오피오이드 남용으로 사망하고 있으며 처방 통증 완화제</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>헤로인 및 펜타닐과 같은 합성 오피오이드의 오용과 중독은 미국 내 공중 보건 뿐만아니라 사회</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>․</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>경제적으로 심각한 영향을 미치고 있음</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>질병 통제 예방 센터는 미국 내 처방전 오피오이드 오용의 총 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;></span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>경제적 부담</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;></span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>이 의료비</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>생산성 저하</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>중독 치료 및 형사 사법 관련 비용을 포함하여 연간 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>785 </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>억 달러인 것으로 추산하고 있음</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>(https://www.drugabuse.gov/drugs-abuse/opioids/opioid-overdose-crisis).</span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>▪ </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>美 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>FDA</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>는 지난달 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>30</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>일 자국의 오피오이드 위기에 대응하는 의료 기기 개발을 장려하기 위해 혁신 과제를 개시함</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. FDA</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>에 따르면</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>이번 과제를 통해 오피오이드 중독 예방</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>감지 및 치료에 도움을 주는 새로운 의료 기술</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>(MedTech) </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>개발을 촉진할 수 있을 것이라 기대함</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>.</span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>▪ </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>해당 혁신과제는 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>FDA Innovation Challenge: Devices to Prevent and Treat Opioid Use Disorder (&ldquo;the Challenge&rdquo; </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>라고 불리우며</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>, CDHR (Center for Devices and Radiological Health)</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>에서 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>6</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>월 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>1</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>일부터 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>9</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>월 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>30</span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>일까지 신청서를 받으며 본 과제에 체택된 의료기기는 </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>FDA </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>와 긴밀한 협력 하에 제품개발 및 검토과정을 거치게 됨</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>. </span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;>▪ </span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>FDA </span><span style=font-size: 11pt;>혁신과제 발표전문 및 과제내용</span><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>: https://www.fda.gov/AboutFDA/CentersOffices/OfficeofMedicalProductsandTobacco/CDRH/CDRHInnovation/ucm609082.htm</span></p><p class=0 style=line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;><span style=letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>[Mass Device, 2018. 5. 30.]</span></p><p class=0 style=text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;><a href=https://www.massdevice.com/fda-medical-device-innovation-challenge-opioid-crisis/><span style=color: rgb(0, 0, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;>https://www.massdevice.com/fda-medical-device-innovation-challenge-opioid-crisis/</span></a></p><p class=0><span style=font-family: 한컴바탕;></span></p>".replace(/(<([^>]+)>)/gi, "");        <input id="matrixKhtml10" name="matrixKhtml10" type="hidden" value='&lt;p&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;!--StartFragment--&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;의료 서비스&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;미국 메디케이드 비용 증가 지속으로 각 주별 예산 압박 예상&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.5pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;피치&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Fich)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의 최근 보고서에 따르면&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의료서비스와 연금에 할당되는 주정부 및 지역 예산&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(state &amp;amp; local budgets)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2025&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년까지 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;800% &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;오를 것으로 예측&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의료와 연금 예산이 증가함에 따라 다른 분야 즉 교육&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;교통&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;안전&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;주거 및 환경 분야 등의 예산 축소 또는 프로그램에 있어서의 변화가 예상&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.5pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;미국 내 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;7&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;천&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;6&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;백&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;십만명 이상 인구가 메디케이드 수혜를 받고 있고&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;또 메디케이터 확장&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Medicaid expansion)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;으로 인해 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;천&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;5&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;백&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;십만명 이상이 의료보험을 받았음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이들 중 다수는 전에는 메디케이드 수혜자가 아니었음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;즉 프로그램 확대에 따라 주정부도 동일 레벨의 연방&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;/&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;주 프로그램에 예산을 배정하기 위해 노력했음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. 2005&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년부터 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2015&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 사이에 예산 지출비율에 있어서 가장 높은 동력이 의료분야인데&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;수치로는 연간 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;5,860&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;억 달러에서부터 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;9,290&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;억달러로 의료예산이 증가했음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.5pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의료분야 예산 폭증과 더불어 베이비부머세대&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(1940&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;-1960&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년대세대&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의 은퇴와 연금비용 증가로 인해&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;주정부는 균형예산을 위해 노력 중&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;피치 예측치에 따르면 의료와 사회서비스분야 예산은 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2015&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 전체 예산 상 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;30.7%&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;를 차지했지만&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, 2025&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년에는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;38.3%&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;로 증가할 것&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;캘리포니아&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;코네티컷&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;일리노이&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;켄터키&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;루지애나&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;뉴저지와 펜실베니아 등의 주는 상황이 더 좋지 않음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;가장 먼저&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;켄터키주는 이미 메디케이드 지출을 줄이기 위해 노동 요건을 변경하는 정책을 시행하고 있음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;노동 요건이외에도 등록자 수를 줄이기 위하여 수혜 조건 포기&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;소급 적용 커버리지 낮춤&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;기본 보험료 부과&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;총 수혜기간 제한 도입 등&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;), &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;수혜 기간 제한 축소 등을 도입&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;피치는 이 보고서에서 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;10&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년 시나리오 분석을 했는데&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이는 의료와 연금 비용이 향후 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;7&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년간 예산에 어떤 영향을 줄 것인지를 파악하기 위함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. 2025&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;년까지 예산을 늘리려면 세금을 올리거나 메디케이드 또는 다른 프로그램 지출을 줄여야 하는데 주요 공교육과 수송분야가 공격분야가 될 것으로 예상&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[Healthcaredive, 2018.6.14.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.healthcaredive.com/news/fitch-says-medicaid-cost-growth-likely-to-force-states-to-cut-programs/525652/"&gt;&lt;span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;https://www.healthcaredive.com/news/fitch-says-medicaid-cost-growth-likely-to-force-states-to-cut-programs/525652/&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;제약&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;] FDA, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;신설 의회 입법&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;(On right to try)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;에 적극 대응함에도 불구하고 디테일 부족&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;5&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;30&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;일 트럼프 대통령이 사인한 신설 법&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(On right to try)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;은 생명위협 질환에 걸린 환자&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;기 승인 치료 옵션을 다 써버렸고 임상시험에 참가할 수 없는 환자가 임상&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;상을 마친 시험약에 접근할 수 있도록 시험약 생산자와 직접 거래할 수 있도록 함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;미 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;국장 고틀리&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Scott Gottlieb)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;6&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월 초 보스턴에서 열린 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;Bio US&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에 참석하여 신법의 지지자 및 비판자들과 함께 자문을 계속할 것을 약속&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;현재 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;라첼 셔먼&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;수석 부국장&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이 이끄는 내부그룹이 새로운 가이드&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;규정&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, Q&amp;amp;A &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;등을 포함하는 제안을 준비 중이라고 함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;신설 연방법률의 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;채택과 제도화는 찬반양론을 모두 고려하면서 진행할 것이므로 당분간 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의 계획은 명확하게 드러나지 않을 것임&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;현재 라첼 셔먼이 주도하에 현재 워킹그룹을 만들어 운영하고 있는데&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;컨설팅 사무소&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;제약과 바이오직스 센타 등의 대표들도 그룹 안에 포함될 것&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. FDA&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;는 이 법률 하에서의 시험약의 사용과 관련된 임상결과치를 사용해서 승인을 지연하거나 하는 등 실제 승인에 영향을 끼치게 하지는 않을 것임&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;물론 그 결과치가 약의 안전성 또는 스폰서의 사용 요청을 결정하는데 중요한 경우라면 달라질 수 있음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;췌장암 환자를 위한 임상시험약을 가진 중소기업은 실제로 이 법에 따른 접근에 대한 문의를 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;10&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;통이나 받았다고 함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;관련 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;2&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;개 중소기업은 회사의 시험약을 새로운 연방법 하에서 사전 접근을 부여하지 않을 것이라 함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;현재 상황에서는 기업의 최종 목표와도 일치하지 않고 그럴 필요성도 못 느끼기 때문&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;CDER(Center for Drug Evaluation and Research) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;직원들도 이에 대한 대응 교육을 받고 있으나 현재까지 실질적인 도움이 되고 있지는 않다&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;왜냐하면 론 존슨&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Ron Johnson) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;상원위원의 발언에 따르면&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이 신법은 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에 추가로 더 권한을 주는 법이 아니라 환자들에게 생명에 대한 희망을 주기위해 오히려 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;권한을 축소하는 것이기 때문&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[Pinksheet, 2018. 6. 13.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;a href="https://pink.pharmaintelligence.informa.com/PS123273/US-FDAs-Plan-On-Right-To-Try-Big-On-Congressional-Engagement-Short-On-Policy-Details"&gt;&lt;span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;https://pink.pharmaintelligence.informa.com/PS123273/US-FDAs-Plan-On-Right-To-Try-Big-On-Congressional-Engagement-Short-On-Policy-Details&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;헬스 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;IT] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;구글&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;음성인식 활용하여 전자의무기록 생성에 도전 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;CNBC &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;리포트에 따르면 구글이 이른바 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;"&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;차세대 임상 방문 경험&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(next gen clinical visit experience)" &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;프로그램개발을 목표로 개발팀을 새로이 구성 할 계획&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이번 팀은 이미 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;Stanford Medical&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;과 협력 하에 인공 지능과 음성 인식을 통해 전자의무기록&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(EHR)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;을 생성하는 것에 대한 기능 평가를 하고 있으며 본 프로젝트의 초점은 음성 인식을 사용하여 의사가 메모를 작성하는 데 도움이 될 수 있도록 하는 것임&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;최근 연구에 따르면 일차 진료 의사&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Primary care doctor)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;는 근무일 기준으로 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;EHR &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;및 컴퓨터 작업에 업무 시간 절반 이상을 소비하는 것으로 나타났음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;본 연구를 주도한 스탠포드&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Stanford) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;의사 스티븐 린 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Steven Lin)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;은 이번 개발에서 가장 큰 남점은 정확성을 지키는 것이며 이 부분이 해결된다면 불필요한 행정 업무를 줄이고 의사와 환자 간 대면시간을 늘릴 수 있을 것이라고 전함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[HealthcareDive, 2018. 6. 15.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.healthcaredive.com/news/google-seeking-talent-in-voice-tech-to-improve-doctor-patient-experience/525757/"&gt;&lt;span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;https://www.healthcaredive.com/news/google-seeking-talent-in-voice-tech-to-improve-doctor-patient-experience/525757/&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;헬스 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;IT] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;美&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;의료업계&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;블록체인 기술 활용한 의료제공자 데이터 품질 관리에 주목 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;최근 발표된 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;EY&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;와 휴마나&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Humana) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;백서에 따르면 블록체인과 같은 분산 원장 기술을 통해 비용과 중복 데이터 가능성은 낮추되 의료 서비스 제공자&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(Provider) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;데이터의 품질을 향상 시킬 수 있다고 전함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;본 보고서에 따르면 의료 서비스 제공자 데이터 관리와 같은 일상적인 행정 활동을 개선하는 것이 의료 산업의 비효율성과 낭비를 줄이는 첫 단계일 수 있으며 미국 의료기관은 매년 의료 서비스 제공자 데이터를 유지하는 데 약 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;21 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;억 달러를 지출하며 그 중 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;75 %&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;가 중복된 데이터 인 것으로 나타남&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이러한 상황이 야기된 원인 중 하나는 의료소비자 및 기타 업계의 이해 관계자가 얽힌 상태에서 상호간 데이터 교환 없이 데이터가 저장되기 때문임&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이러한 상황에서 블록체인 기술은 사용자간 데이터 교환을 허용하고 여러 이해 관계자를 연결할 수 있는 기회를 제공함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;한편&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;美 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;대형 의료서비스 기업인 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;Humana&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;는 이미 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;MultiPlan, UnitedHealth Group&amp;lsquo;S Optum, UnitedHealthcare &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;및 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;Quest Diagnostics&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;와 협력하여 의료 제공자 네트워크 목록을 수정하기 위한 블록체인 파일럿 프로젝트를 진행 중&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[HealthcareDive, 2018. 6. 11.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.healthcaredive.com/news/fixing-provider-directories-a-low-risk-way-to-test-blockchain-report-sugge/525363/"&gt;&lt;span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;https://www.healthcaredive.com/news/fixing-provider-directories-a-low-risk-way-to-test-blockchain-report-sugge/525363/&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;&lt;br&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;[&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;의료기기&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;] &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;美 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;FDA, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;오피오이드 위기 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;(Opioid Crisis) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt; font-weight: bold;"&gt;대응을 위한 의료기기 혁신 과제의 수행 개시&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;미국에서는 매일 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;115&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;명이 넘는 사람들이 오피오이드 남용으로 사망하고 있으며 처방 통증 완화제&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;헤로인 및 펜타닐과 같은 합성 오피오이드의 오용과 중독은 미국 내 공중 보건 뿐만아니라 사회&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;․&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;경제적으로 심각한 영향을 미치고 있음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;질병 통제 예방 센터는 미국 내 처방전 오피오이드 오용의 총 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;"&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;경제적 부담&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;"&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이 의료비&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;생산성 저하&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;중독 치료 및 형사 사법 관련 비용을 포함하여 연간 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;785 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;억 달러인 것으로 추산하고 있음&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(https://www.drugabuse.gov/drugs-abuse/opioids/opioid-overdose-crisis).&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;美 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;는 지난달 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;30&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;일 자국의 오피오이드 위기에 대응하는 의료 기기 개발을 장려하기 위해 혁신 과제를 개시함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. FDA&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에 따르면&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;이번 과제를 통해 오피오이드 중독 예방&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;감지 및 치료에 도움을 주는 새로운 의료 기술&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;(MedTech) &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;개발을 촉진할 수 있을 것이라 기대함&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;해당 혁신과제는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA Innovation Challenge: Devices to Prevent and Treat Opioid Use Disorder (&amp;ldquo;the Challenge&amp;rdquo; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;라고 불리우며&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;, CDHR (Center for Devices and Radiological Health)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;에서 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;6&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;일부터 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;9&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;월 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;30&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;일까지 신청서를 받으며 본 과제에 체택된 의료기기는 &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;와 긴밀한 협력 하에 제품개발 및 검토과정을 거치게 됨&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 140%; text-indent: -9.4pt; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 6px; margin-left: 12px; tab-stops: left blank 48.3pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;▪ &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;FDA &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-size: 11pt;"&gt;혁신과제 발표전문 및 과제내용&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;: https://www.fda.gov/AboutFDA/CentersOffices/OfficeofMedicalProductsandTobacco/CDRH/CDRHInnovation/ucm609082.htm&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="line-height: 107%; letter-spacing: 0pt; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px;"&gt;&lt;span style="letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;[Mass Device, 2018. 5. 30.]&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0" style="text-align: left; line-height: 107%; font-size: 11pt; margin-bottom: 10px; -ms-word-break: keep-all;"&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.massdevice.com/fda-medical-device-innovation-challenge-opioid-crisis/"&gt;&lt;span style="color: rgb(0, 0, 255); letter-spacing: 0pt; font-family: 굴림; font-size: 11pt;"&gt;https://www.massdevice.com/fda-medical-device-innovation-challenge-opioid-crisis/&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p class="0"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: 한컴바탕;"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;'/>

      <!-- 식사구성평가  -->
      <h2 class="box_title">
       <a href="#stage_set08" id="stage_set08A">
        식사구성평가
       </a>
      </h2>
      <div class="tabcontent rolypoly" id="stage_set08">
       <div class="float_left">
        <img alt="물, 우유 및 유제품류, 과일류, 고기 생선 계란 두부, 채소류, 곡류" src="/resources/images/kps/main/rolypoly.gif"/>
       </div>
       <div class="float_right">
        <h3 class="tit_subject">
         식사구성
         <span>
          오뚝이
         </span>
        </h3>
        <p class="info">
         <span>
          식사구성오뚝이는 한국인 영양섭취기준(한국영양학회, 2010)에서 제안하는 대상별 권장식사패턴을 인지하고 실천할 수 있도록 식사구성가이드를 도식화한 모델입니다.
         </span>
         식사구성오뚝이는 하루동안 섭취하면 좋은 식품군 1회 분량 섭취횟수가 몸통에 표현되어 있습니다.
        </p>
        <ul class="boxlist">
         <li>
          <a href="http://www.khidi.or.kr/board?menuId=MENU01558" target="_blank" title="새창으로 열림">
           <i class="icon1101">
           </i>
           식사구성 가이드 개요
          </a>
         </li>
         <li>
          <a href="http://www.khidi.or.kr/board?menuId=MENU01559" target="_blank" title="새창으로 열림">
           <i class="icon1102">
           </i>
           음식구분표
          </a>
         </li>
         <li>
          <a href="http://www.khidi.or.kr/board?menuId=MENU01560" target="_blank" title="새창으로 열림">
           <i class="icon1103">
           </i>
           식사구성 오뚝이
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </div>
      </div>

      <!-- 건강위험도평가 -->
      <h2 class="box_title nutrition_title">
       <a href="#stage_set09" id="stage_set09A">
        건강위험도평가
       </a>
      </h2>
      <div class="tabcontent nutrition" id="stage_set09">
       <div class="float_wrap">
        <div class="float_left">
         <h3 class="tit_subject">
          건강위험도
          <span>
           평가
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p class="info">
          <span>
           영양관리를 위한 식생활 중심의 건강위험도를 평가하는 도구입니다.
          </span>
          개인의 식생활 진단을 통해 만성질환 위험도를 평가하고, 그 결과에 근거하여 식생활 습관 개선을 도와주는 도구로써 국내에서는 최초로 개발되었습니다.
         </p>
        </div>
        <ul class="number_list">
         <li>
          <strong class="numTitle">
           건강위험도 평가 하기
          </strong>

            </a>

           <li>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      $(document).ready(function() {
	
	var subject = "#"+$('#cookieSubject').val();//선호정보 선택 쿠키값
	
	$(".tabcontent").hide();
	$(subject).fadeIn();
	
	$(".stage_setArea h2 > a").removeClass("on");
	$(subject+"A").addClass("on");

	//선호정보 미선택시 첫번째 탭을 보여준다.
	if(subject=="#"){
		$("#stage_set01A").addClass("on");
		$("#stage_set01").fadeIn();
	}
	
	$(".stage_setArea h2").click(function() {
		$(".stage_setArea h2 > a").removeClass("on");
		$(this).find("a").addClass("on");
		$(".tabcontent").hide();
		var activeTab = $(this).find("a").attr("href");
		$(activeTab).fadeIn();
		return false;
	});
	
	$(".btn_stageSet > button").click(function(){
		$(".subject_setting").show();
		return false;
	});

	$(".subject_setting .btn_close").click(function(){
		$(".subject_setting").hide();
		$(".btn_stageSet button").focus();
		return false;
	});
});

function fnAlertPrepare(){
	alert("준비중입니다.");
	return;
}

function fnNewsLatterForm(){
	var strStyle = "resizable=yes";
	var sleft = (screen.width - 870) / 2;
	var stop = (screen.height - 710) / 2;
	var style = "left="+sleft+",top="+stop+",width=870,height=710,"+strStyle;
	
	var pop_title = "viewContent";
	window.open("", pop_title,style);

	var frmData = document.frmDataNews;
	frmData.menuId.value="MENU01031";
	frmData.action = "/joinNewsLetter/form";
	frmData.target = pop_title;
	frmData.submit();
}
     </script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     var ObjScrollingWeeklyHot = new ScrollingWeeklyHot("WeeklyHot-Wrapper", '', 'a'); // WeeklyHot Scrolling
var ObjScrollingGuide = new ScrollingGuide("Guide-Wrapper", '', 'img'); // Guide Scrolling


//라디오,체크박스
(function(){
	$.fn.customRadioCheck = function() {
		return this.each(function() {
			var $this = $(this);
			var $span = $('<span/>');
			$span.addClass('custom-'+ ($this.is(':checkbox') ? 'check' : 'radio'));
			$this.is(':checked') && $span.addClass('checked'); // init
			$span.insertAfter($this);
			$this.parent('li').addClass('custom-label').attr('onclick', ''); // Fix clicking label in iOS
			// hide by shifting left
			// Events
						
			$this.on({
				change: function() {
					if ($this.is(':radio')) {
						$this.parent().parent().siblings('li').find('.custom-radio').removeClass('checked');
					}
					$span.toggleClass('checked', $this.is(':checked'));
				}
				//focus: function() { $span.addClass('focus');},
				//blur: function() { $span.removeClass('focus');}
			});
			
		});
	};
}());
$('input[type=checkbox], input[type=radio]').customRadioCheck();
    </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function fnFamilySiteClick(){
	var dispalyAttr = $(".link_site").css('display');
	if(dispalyAttr == "none"){
		$(".link_site").css('display', 'block');
	}else{		
		$(".link_site").css('display', 'none');
	}
}

//배너
$(function() {
	
	// 콘텐츠제공서비스 품질인증 레이어팝업
	$("#goodContent").click(function(){
		var obj = $(this).offset();
		$("#goodContentLayer").css("z-index", "99");
		$("#goodContentLayer").css("bottom", "150px");
		$("#goodContentLayer").css("left", obj.left-500+"px");
		$("#goodContentLayer").fadeIn();
	});
	$("#goodContentLayer > img").click(function(){
		$("#goodContentLayer").fadeOut();
	});
	
	try {
		/* 슬라이드 배너 */
		$('#banner_zone').ScrollerSlide
		({
			'target'				: '.banner_list',							/* 슬라이드 영역 obj */
			'display'				: 3,										/* 슬라이드 가능 리스트 수 */
			'delay'					: 1,										/* 딜레이 시간(초) */
			'pause'					: 1,										/* 멈춤 딜레이 시간(초) */
			'direction'				: 'x',										/* 슬라이드 방향 x 좌우, y 위아래 */
			'controlls'				:											/* 슬라이드 컨트롤러  */
			{
				'name'				: '.banner_control',						/* 컨트롤러 영역 obj */
				'play'				: '.btn_play',								/* 슬라이드 시작 버튼명 */
				'pause'			    : '.btn_pause'								/* 슬라이드 멈춤 버튼명 */
			}
		});
	}
	catch (e)
	{
		$.debug(e);
	}
});
   </script>
